    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer13752434934680793729">Survivor... a word continuously thought of when reading this memoir. Upon the release of The Freedom Writers Diary and film adaptation starring Hilary Swank in 2007, New York Times bestselling author Darrius Garrett realized that both book and movie tell the Freedom Writer Story as a whole, but not on a personal level. During speaking engagements, the same questions always</span>
  <span id="freeText13752434934680793729" style="display:none">Survivor... a word continuously thought of when reading this memoir. Upon the release of The Freedom Writers Diary and film adaptation starring Hilary Swank in 2007, New York Times bestselling author Darrius Garrett realized that both book and movie tell the Freedom Writer Story as a whole, but not on a personal level. During speaking engagements, the same questions always surface: 'Did Ms. Gruwell change you? How did you make it out of the gang life? What stopped you from killing yourself?' Darrius's answers are inside.<br /><br />Diary of a Freedom Writer takes you on a journey beyond the classrooms to the treacherous streets of Long Beach, California. An innocent little boy born in poverty and raised in a violent environment, Darrius became a product of the streets, written off by the school and judicial systems alike, growing up in an environment full of gangs and drugs. He spent his life searching for a father figure until he became a Freedom Writer, motivational speaker, bestselling author, and finally a father himself. His story is that of a man realizing his experiences are what made him the man he has been seeking to be all his life. Upon beating the odds, Diary of a Freedom Writer serves as proof that Darrius's story of struggle, life, change, and hope will uplift, educate, encourage, and inspire.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13752434934680793729" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/628278432?book_show_action=true">May 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marcus Anderson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marcus Anderson" href="/user/show/20841496-marcus-anderson">Marcus Anderson</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer628278432" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7918680400444337223">I got the opportunity to read this book as an eBook today. So I made it a point to get on here and give a review. I love this book. My opinion is that its better than the original Book Freedom Writers Diary only because i felt bad for the students in the book,and at times I felt there was unnecessary cursing in some stories; then I watched the movie and became a fan of the Freedom Writers. But mostly I would say that I bonded with the character Marcus as we share the same first name..lol but als</span>
  <span id="freeText7918680400444337223" style="display:none">I got the opportunity to read this book as an eBook today. So I made it a point to get on here and give a review. I love this book. My opinion is that its better than the original Book Freedom Writers Diary only because i felt bad for the students in the book,and at times I felt there was unnecessary cursing in some stories; then I watched the movie and became a fan of the Freedom Writers. But mostly I would say that I bonded with the character Marcus as we share the same first name..lol but also his story was amazing in the movie. Then I received a tweet that Marcus is really the original Freedom Writer Darrius Garrett and the link to his new book. So with much interest I bought the eBook for like $10.00 and I'm glad I did so as it was well worth it. I thought the movie was good but Mr. Garrett book is amazing. What I seen in the movie is small compared to the stories he told in his new book. I am a youth leader here at my community center and I thought of each of my kids as I read Mr. Garrett's story. <br /><br />Great Job Mr. Garrett you get 5 stars from me as well as I will buy a hard copy as well to share this with the young people in my youth group.<br /><br />Keep doing what you are doing sir.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/682884575" />
    <a title="Jamie Robinson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22716564-jamie-robinson"><img alt="Jamie Robinson" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/682884575?book_show_action=true">Aug 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jamie Robinson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jamie Robinson" href="/user/show/22716564-jamie-robinson">Jamie Robinson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">anyone</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer682884575" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18417881376114258719">This was such an enlightening and inspirational book. The author wrote from the heart and I could see the face of "Marcus" from the film as I read this book. The story about his life and the behind the scene story of the Freedom Writer experience was captivating. I have become a true fan of Mr. Garretts writing and plan to tell everyone that I can about how great this book is as I feel this book just as many others will be one of the hands down greatest memoirs written that slip through the crac</span>
  <span id="freeText18417881376114258719" style="display:none">This was such an enlightening and inspirational book. The author wrote from the heart and I could see the face of "Marcus" from the film as I read this book. The story about his life and the behind the scene story of the Freedom Writer experience was captivating. I have become a true fan of Mr. Garretts writing and plan to tell everyone that I can about how great this book is as I feel this book just as many others will be one of the hands down greatest memoirs written that slip through the cracks and stays under the radar because of who the author is as well as the misconception that people will think its just the same story they have read in the previous book and seen in the movie but its so far from the truth.I appreciate the fact that the book didn't have an unlimited amount of cursing in it as you can see the maturity and growth of this young man as the chapters progresses Unlike other books this is authentic and very real. I heard him speak at a conference that I attended a few months ago and he talked about this book and its everything that he said it would be and more. I'm glad I read it and I hope millions of other avid readers pick it up as well. </span>
  <a data-text-id="18417881376114258719" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie ~aka Reading Machine~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie ~aka Reading Machine~" href="/user/show/5573346-angie-aka-reading-machine">Angie ~aka Reading Machine~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition 9781627466813" href="/book/show/18994860-diary-of-a-freedom-writer">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5573346-angie-aka-reading-machine?shelf=first-reads-review-books">first-reads-review-books</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1114948978" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11321230334444741874">Many of us have probably seen the movie The Freedom Writers. Yet how many of us have wonder about the people behind The Freedom Writers. Diary of a Freedom Writer:The Experience takes us on an in depth look into Darrius Garrett's life and how Erin Gruwell helped change not only his life but every member of The Freedom Writers. I was always curious about the people behind The Freedom Writers. When Darrius Garrett asked me to review his book I jumped at the opportunity.<br/><br/>I found this book to be a wo</span>
  <span id="freeText11321230334444741874" style="display:none">Many of us have probably seen the movie The Freedom Writers. Yet how many of us have wonder about the people behind The Freedom Writers. Diary of a Freedom Writer:The Experience takes us on an in depth look into Darrius Garrett's life and how Erin Gruwell helped change not only his life but every member of The Freedom Writers. I was always curious about the people behind The Freedom Writers. When Darrius Garrett asked me to review his book I jumped at the opportunity.<br /><br />I found this book to be a wonderful addition to The Freedom Writer movie. I learned that everyday people can be truly special and remarkable in their own right too. Diary of a Freedom Writer:The Experience takes you on a journey of self-discovery, hope, lost, heart break, and most of all happiness in yourself. Definitely reading this book has made me look at my own life and wonder~Can I dare to dream too? The answer is yes I can dream too.<br /><br />I'll admit I'm usually not a fan of biographies but I found this one too compelling not to read. I've asked myself several questions and now I'm going to be searching for the answers to those questions. I highly recommend this book to anyone who is curious about The Freedom Writers. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11321230334444741874" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer627840721" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2527977464038066900">I received this book as part of a Goodreads First Reads giveaway. I was already familiar with the Freedom Writers' story having seen the movie and also having had the opportunity to see Manuel Scott speak at an orientation for teachers. Darrius Garrett's book presents a fresh perspective on the story and allows you to take a walk in the life of one of the Freedom Writers. Not only does he take you into Erin Gruwell's classroom, but also offers you a behind the scenes look at what his life was li</span>
  <span id="freeText2527977464038066900" style="display:none">I received this book as part of a Goodreads First Reads giveaway. I was already familiar with the Freedom Writers' story having seen the movie and also having had the opportunity to see Manuel Scott speak at an orientation for teachers. Darrius Garrett's book presents a fresh perspective on the story and allows you to take a walk in the life of one of the Freedom Writers. Not only does he take you into Erin Gruwell's classroom, but also offers you a behind the scenes look at what his life was like outside the classroom. His writing allows you to truly put yourself in his shoes and imagine what you would do in the situations he faces throughout the book. I would recommend this book to anyone interested in the Freedom Writers' story especially other educators. It reminds us how important it can be to look beyond what we see in the classroom and to consider how a student's home life can impact their school experience. </span>
  <a data-text-id="2527977464038066900" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1349134186" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1349134186" />
    <a title="Shereen Rafea" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31585099-shereen-rafea"><img alt="Shereen Rafea" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574771486p2/31585099.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1349134186?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shereen Rafea" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shereen Rafea" href="/user/show/31585099-shereen-rafea">Shereen Rafea</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1349134186" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13210209700079421883">Raw, simple and honest. LOVED IT. Facts: this book is a memoir (not a diary) of one of the Freedom Writers ( see movie), Darrius. It tells the story of a boy growing up under the influence of drugs and gang violence. Then he meets a teacher who changes his life forever. While the movie focused on the teacher and the class, this book is Darrius's chance to tell the world more of his personal story. Terrific result. A fast, yet effective read. Darrius describes each stage in his life like a camera</span>
  <span id="freeText13210209700079421883" style="display:none">Raw, simple and honest. LOVED IT. Facts: this book is a memoir (not a diary) of one of the Freedom Writers ( see movie), Darrius. It tells the story of a boy growing up under the influence of drugs and gang violence. Then he meets a teacher who changes his life forever. While the movie focused on the teacher and the class, this book is Darrius's chance to tell the world more of his personal story. Terrific result. A fast, yet effective read. Darrius describes each stage in his life like a camera zooming in on important milestones and moments. He adds bursts of creativity here and there with poetry and reflections. While the style did not always seem in-sync to me (past tense voice clashing with present tense) , this little book is a beautiful story of surviving , perseverance and tolerance .. Oh and of course it's about the power of a great teacher :) </span>
  <a data-text-id="13210209700079421883" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1538044692" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1538044692" />
    <a title="Jan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22004574-jan"><img alt="Jan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600509223p2/22004574.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1538044692?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jan" href="/user/show/22004574-jan">Jan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22004574-jan?shelf=operation">operation</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22004574-jan?shelf=african-american-experience">african-american-experience</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22004574-jan?shelf=american">american</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22004574-jan?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22004574-jan?shelf=memoir-biography">memoir-biography</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22004574-jan?shelf=nonfiction">nonfiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22004574-jan?shelf=ya">ya</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1538044692" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11990207293897341059">Very moving memoir of Darrius Garrett, one of the freedom writers from the movie of the same name. The writing is often awkward and ungrammatical, but Darrius' voice rings strong and true as he speaks of his life growing up surrounded by drugs, danger, and poor self-esteem. He vividly paints his journey from a scared and angry kid to the kind, gentle and inspirational man he is now. I shed a few tears during my read, out of sorrow, then out of power of his inspiration. Thank you, Darrius. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('u1/l+oIlU4FGbIsnuOK8rXhYkbRRrfahlFadCFjZ9y58f1nvEdUnhRGP7bOLSCNc0vnsqjpKNU3VVDTsDOcssw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer2267206822481269339">In a few short years, author, songwriter, motivational speaker and freedom writer Darrius Garrett transitioned from the ’hood to humanitarian, reaching heights he once could only imagine. As an inner-city youth of Long Beach, Calif., Garrett could easily have become a product of his environment but rose instead to become a pillar of his community. He became a New York Times bestselling author at a</span>
  <span id="freeText2267206822481269339" style="display:none">In a few short years, author, songwriter, motivational speaker and freedom writer Darrius Garrett transitioned from the ’hood to humanitarian, reaching heights he once could only imagine. As an inner-city youth of Long Beach, Calif., Garrett could easily have become a product of his environment but rose instead to become a pillar of his community. He became a New York Times bestselling author at a young age when he co-wrote The Freedom Writers Diary, which inspired the 2007 movie The Freedom Writers starring Hilary Swank. In the film, Garrett was portrayed as the heart-wrenching character Marcus. He also wrote the song “Change” for the movie’s soundtrack.<br /><br />As a freedom writer, Garrett was co-recipient of the Spirit of Anne Frank Award, the Crystal Apple Award and other honors. He has shared his story with the likes of Miep Gies, the Dutch woman who hid Anne Frank; former U.S. Secretary of Education Richard Riley; and singer/actor/activist Harry Belafonte. The story has also been featured on segments on Primetime Live with Connie Chung, The Oprah Winfrey Show and NPR, as well as in articles in the L.A. Times, the Long Beach Press-Telegram and the Associated Press. Garrett’s recent works include a book of poetry titled Poetic Thoughts and the soon-to-be-published Diary of a Freedom Writer: The Experience. He frequently speaks to at-risk youth in schools and detention centers, as well as educators, social workers, businesspeople and politicians. Motivating his audiences with his story of hope, tolerance and action, Garrett encourages them to become the fire that ignites change.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2267206822481269339" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        script.src = load[i];
        first.parentNode.insertBefore(script, first);
      }
    }
  if (w.attachEvent) {
    w.attachEvent('onload', go);
  } else {
    w.addEventListener('load', go, false);
  }
}(window, document,
    ['//assets.pinterest.com/js/pinit.js',
     '//apis.google.com/js/plusone.js'
    ]
  ));

//]]>
</script>

      </div>

    </div>
